822026-03-08T22:09:34.886287agentmessage-
The `answer.json` has been written at `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/answer.json`. Here is a summary of everything captured:

---

## What the answer covers

### 33 source files documented across 4 functional areas

---

### 1. INI File Parser

The INI parsing is built on `gopkg.in/ini.v1` and orchestrated through a chain of functions in **`pkg/setting/setting.go`**:

| Function | Line | Role |
|---|---|---|
| `loadConfiguration` | 963 | Master pipeline: loads `defaults.ini`, merges `custom.ini`, applies overrides, calls `expandConfig` |
| `loadSpecifiedConfigFile` | 922 | Merges `custom.ini` (or `--config` path) into the master `*ini.File` |
| `parseINIFile` | 1165 | Stores merged file in `cfg.Raw`, dispatches to all `read*Settings` functions |
| `NewCfgFromBytes` | 1100 | Creates `Cfg` from raw INI bytes |
| `NewCfgFromINIFile` | 1116 | Creates `Cfg` from an already-parsed `*ini.File` |

**`conf/defaults.ini`** (2244 lines) is the canonical source of all default values — it is always loaded first.

---

### 2. Environment Variable Override Logic

Two distinct mechanisms:

**Startup-time** (`applyEnvVariableOverrides`, line 748): iterates every section+key in the merged `*ini.File`, computes `GF_<SECTION>_<KEY>` via `EnvKey()` (line 855), calls `os.Getenv`, and overwrites the key if non-empty.

**Runtime** (`DynamicSection` / `SectionWithEnvOverrides`, lines 1567–1609): wraps a section so that each `Key()` call re-checks the environment at call time. Used by `[auth.extended_jwt]` and `[auth.passwordless]`. Backed by the `osutil.Env` interface (`pkg/util/osutil/osutil.go`) for testability.

**`pkg/setting/expanders.go`** handles a third layer — interpolation tokens (`${ENV_VAR}`, `$__file{/path}`, `$__env{VAR}`) inside INI values, resolved after all overrides are applied.
